***катапульта.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катапульта.html>катапу́льта</a> (23296)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">catapulta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катапульта.html>катапу́льта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katapúlʹta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катапульта.html>катапу́льты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катапульта.html>катапу́льты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катапульта.html>катапу́льт</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>catapult <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">medieval siege-warfare device</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катастрофа.html>катастро́фа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katastrófa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катастрофа.html>катастро́фа</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">katastrófa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***катать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a> (11268)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покатать.html>поката́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive (a trolley), to take (somebody) for a drive</li>
<li>to ride (on a bicycle, on a swing, etc.)</li>
<li>to roll <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to cause to revolve</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is in the class of Russian abstract verbs. Its counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>/<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">катну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покатить.html>покати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are concrete verbs.
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тать.html>та́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:покатать.html>поката́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кат-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***кататься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a> (4640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покататься.html>поката́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ride <i>in a vehicle</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>лю́бишь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> са́ночки <a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ljúbišʹ <b>katátʹsja</b>, ljubí i sánočki vozítʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">after the feast comes the reckoning</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">if you like to ride, you should like to pull the sleigh</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to roll <i>(abstract verb), see</i> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>кати́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыр</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сле</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak syr v másle <b>katátʹsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to live in clover</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">to roll like cheese in butter</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́ху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>katátʹsja</b> so sméxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to split one's sides with laughter, to roar with laughter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ride <i>on skis, skates, bicycle, or snowboard</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Katátʹsja</b> na lýžax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ski</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тать.html>та́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:покататься.html>поката́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кат-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***катафалк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лк</a> (28340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">catafalque</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">catafalco</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*catafalicum</i>, probably derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κατά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fala</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scaffolding, wooden siege tower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katafálk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катафалк.html>катафа́лков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>catafalque, catafalco</li>
<li>hearse, bier</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:категорически.html>категори́чески</a> (4977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:категорически.html>категори́чески</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kategoríčeski</span>)

<ol><li>categorically</li>
<li>flatly, strongly, out of hand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:категорически.html>категори́чески</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:возражать.html>возража́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kategoríčeski</b> vozražátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">strongly object</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:категорически.html>категори́чески</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвергать.html>отверга́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kategoríčeski</b> otvergátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reject vigorously</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***катер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>ка́тер</a> (4726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cutter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>ка́тер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">káter</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>ка́тера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>катера́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катер.html>катеро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> motorboat, boat <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">with an inboard engine</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cutter</li></ol>

***катить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a> (1654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">катити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kotiti</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покатить.html>покати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll, to push <i>(some object with wheels)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бочок.html>бо́чку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>katítʹ</b> bóčku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">turn in, blow the whistle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drive <i>(quickly)</i></li>
<li><i>(a car etc.)</i> to bowl along</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покатить.html>покати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are Russian concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каталка.html>ката́лка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">katálka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ка́танка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kátanka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">качение</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kačenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>кати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покатиться.html>покати́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rush, to tear</li>
<li>to sweep, to move, to flow, to stream, to roll
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёзы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>кати́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sljózy <b>katílisʹ</b> po jejó ščekám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tears were rolling down her cheeks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>ка́тится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>днём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">denʹ <b>kátitsja</b> za dnjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">day after day rolls by</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>кати́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>katísʹ</b> otsjúda!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">get out!, clear off!, beat it!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катиться.html>кати́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покатиться.html>покати́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokatítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are Russian concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.

<p><b>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:покатиться.html>покати́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кат-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каток.html>като́к</a> (9776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кататься.html>ката́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to skate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каток.html>като́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">katók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каток.html>катка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каток.html>катки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каток.html>катко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>skating rink, ice rink</li>
<li>steamroller, road roller, roller <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">compactor-type engineering vehicle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
